At first it was a strong like, then a love, then I bought a bottle, and it was a terrible ownership experience. My bottle would leak when traveling, and even just by car for a few hours. I'm not alone in this. I've seen others online complain of the same leakage issues.<br />
After fighting with Louis Vuitton, I finally got them to agree to replace the bottle. The replacement bottle also leaked, although not as bad as the first. The performance of the replacement bottle was also horrendous. It was a skin scent almost immediately, and I felt like it didn't smell as good as I remembered. I don't know how much of it, though, was my souring on LV perfumes as a result of the poor product quality here or the insanely lacking customer service until I finally found the right person willing to work with me.<br />
I'm sending the bottle back for store credit. I'll have to pick out another LV scent, although I'm a bit nervous whether the bottle will leak. I never had that issue with Afternoon Swim or Cactus Garden--both of which I still adore.<br />
I think there's something different about these bottles in particular vs the others. Maybe the tolerances of this bottle are just slightly off, causing the leakage.<br />
I've owned at least 160 bottles of fragrance in my lifetime to date, definitely over 300 if you include samples. I have NEVER had anything leak like these bottles. This is absolutely unacceptable. For a now whopping $330 (plus tax) price point, this is obscene.<br />
I've never had a fragrance go from such a "love" to "huge pass" so fast.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81423"comment_id="2313432"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Pacific-Chill-81423.html?ccid=2313432#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2313211" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Louis Vuitton does a great job making their colognes smell real and not synthetic like some others when wearing this fragrance, you can have the confidence of saying that you smell the best in the room always, and it will never be overpowering. The only slight issue with this fragrance is that it is 300 bucks which is a little bit much considering I don't think scented alcohol should be 300 bucks in any case, but this is one of them that would be worth the money I would pay 400 bucks for it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; <br />
Wow.<br />
<br />
I tried it today in the Louis Vitton store in Athens, Greece. <br />
<br />
A blast of exotic fruits , a tremendous smell that travels you to the Greek Islands while sipping cocktails in front of the sea in the breeze.<br />
<br />
The type of fragrance that you will wear for one summer only and will associate itself with the monumental times and memories that you will make for the rest of your life. A fantastic "bottlification" of the sentence "summer holidays in the Aegean Sea".<br />
<br />
Thr type of fragrance that you will meet someone for a summer fling and the smell of it will bring you back to the carefree days.<br />
<br />
But, it reminded me of something I have smelled before. I spend the entire day thinking about it untill I went to shower.<br />
<br />
And then it dawned me. This is the fragrance that "Old Spice" copied to make the limited edition "The White Wolf" shampoo as a "Netflix Special". <br />
<br />
I literally have them right next to each other and they are almost identical.<br />
<br />
For anyone wanting the shampoo version, try to find the Old Spice special. When I use it for showering, the entire house smells like Pacific Chill. I think though its discontinued atm at least here in Greece.<br />
<br />
9/10 fragrance, a summer &amp; a passing love that you will never forget.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81423"comment_id="2239789"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Pacific-Chill-81423.html?ccid=2239789#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2239544" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; But this combo is so expensive probably only a few can actually try this.<br />
<br />
Layer this with Imagination - Imagination first, then Pacific Chill. I discovered this by accident when I went to the LV store and sprayed the two on two testing cards, and put them in my pocket. It sat there for about half a day and when I got home, I pulled out a blast of an absolutely phenomenal scent.<br />
<br />
There is some incredible synergy between the Soap+Chinese Black Tea in Imagination and the sweet citrus and apricot in Pacific Chill. It helps that delicious Pacific Chill scent that we all love last a lot longer.<br />
<br />
In fact, that layer was the reason why I ended up buying both Imagination and Pacific Chill (initially I was just thinking of buying PC).<br />
<br />
Yes, you can thank me in a PM if you REALLY want to. üôÑ</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81423"comment_id="2229136"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Pacific-Chill-81423.html?ccid=2229136#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2229123" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This fragrance smells like a tropical mixed drink. The citrus, which is very sour and sweet mixes beautifully with the basil and mint which make the fragrance VERY refreshing. This is the definition of a high heat vacation fragrance.  <br />
<br />
There are some fragrances in my collection that smell amazing but also effect your mood and stir up past memories and emotions. Pacific Chill is one of those fragrances. When wearing this fragrance I am immediately transported to a tropical luxury resort. You are seated poolside sipping on a delicious cocktail while a refreshing breeze blows through. You forget about the worries of the working world and the only thing left to do is chill. <br />
<br />
This is the most refreshing fragrance on the market. Even though LV is a designer house I would consider this fragrance of niche quality! Get out to a LV near you and give this a smell!<br />
<br />
Projection: 7/10<br />
Longevity: 7/10<br />
Smell: 10/10<br />
Price: 4/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81423"comment_id="2225442"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Pacific-Chill-81423.html?ccid=2225442#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2225244" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Lasts a few hours shorter than I would like, regardless this is worth all the money even if you have to spray 10% or 15% of the bottle per wear. Just made it to my top 10 out of the 70+ bottles in my collection.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81423"comment_id="2223708"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Pacific-Chill-81423.html?ccid=2223708#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2223447" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This fragrance is a burst of clean and citrus that is suitable for men and women. I am female, and I absolutely love it. While the scent itself is good, the longevity could have been better. I didn't apply the fragrance until I got to work because it was very humid outside. Within 10 minutes of spraying it, I walked down the hall and received 2 compliments. My co worker wanted to try it so I let her use it. After about 2 1/2 hours, neither of us could smell it on our skin or clothes. For this reason, I can't justify the price to buy a full bottle. I will more than likely get a dupe from DUA or Alexandria Fragrances</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81423"comment_id="2202312"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Pacific-Chill-81423.html?ccid=2202312#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2202115" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I guess I'm lucky that there is a Louis Vuitton store near me, because it's so fun to go there and try out their fragrances!  I was nervous to even walk in there the first time, but after I found someone to ask about the fragrances, it was way more laid back.  She told me that I could try them out as much as I wanted, and spray them on the cards; it was way more laid back than other stores like Ulta, Sephora, Macy's, or Nordstrom!  I didn't buy anything that day, but I thought about it and researched, and then I went back a couple weeks later, determined to buy a bottle.<br />
<br />
So that time, I tried a few fragrances, and decided on Pacific Chill.  I loved the citrus and green apple aroma right from the first smell, and I was especially excited when the guy there told me about how I can get it refilled there for $100 cheaper than a new bottle!  He also hooked me up with a couple free samples, after I asked.  I got Ombre Nomade and L'immensite samples that time.  I felt pretty cool walking through the mall, carrying the Louis Vuitton bag too.<br />
<br />
I've gone back three more times since then, and bought Ombre Nomade, Attrape-Reves, and the new LV LOVERS.  I have a total of ten free samples now, including Afternoon Swim, Imagination, Fleur du Desert, Les Sables Roses, two Ombre Nomade, Material Noire, Attrape-Reves, Rose des Vents, and the L'immensite I already mentioned.  I'm not eve bougie; Louis Vuitton just has amazing fragrances and customer service.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81423"comment_id="2202115"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Pacific-Chill-81423.html?ccid=2202115#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2201663" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It's got the same underlying fuzz of Afternoon Swim, but it's much sweeter and much less focused. On me, the apricot is the dominant note, and I actually get a vague similarity to the original 2019 formulation of Dodo by Zoologist, just without the stank and the photorealistic bird feather note. Anyway, I do like this, but I think it leans quite young. I feel like if you're 18-25 or so, that's sorta the prime zone for being able to pull this off. And although it's 100% unisex, it's not really masculine in any way, if that makes sense.<br />
<br />
This is an excellent release, and it outperforms Afternoon Swim in terms of staying power. But its additional notes make it less versatile, and more person/situation-specific. As a male in my 30s, Afternoon Swim works better on me, but I'm sure many with fewer years behind them will find this to be a perfectly serviceable option during hotter months</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1218968">Arctic Archer</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-20">05/20/24 15:01</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Easily the best and most interesting of Louis Vuitton's summer scents, Pacific Chill is a standout. <br />
<br />
Following Ellena's modern classification of perfumes, Pacific Chill is clearly a ‚Äònarrative‚Äô scent, intended to tell a story through its blend of notes‚Äîthe story being the relaxed, rejuvenating spirit of summer at a luxury villa by the Pacific.<br />
<br />
Its elegant and delicate composition is a refreshing departure from typical citrus-oriented summer scents. Yes, it certainly has citrus, but it is not a citrus scent as such.<br />
<br />
Unlike the more straightforward and less intriguing options like Louis Vuitton‚Äôs underwhelming Afternoon Swim (extremely elegant, but uninteresting pure citrus), Pacific Chill captivates with a complex blend of hint of citrus, blackcurrant, dates and apricot, underscored by a fresh minty note. This makes it an elegant and fascinating summer scent, something to be expected from master perfumer Jacques Cavallier, who composed this masterpiece.<br />
<br />
Furthermore, it's worth noting that this scent is truly unisex, appealing to anyone seeking a sophisticated summer fragrance. It is quite hard to imagine a scent that would be more unisex.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81423"comment_id="2162370"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Pacific-Chill-81423.html?ccid=2162370#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2159978" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This one grew on me quickly. 135+ bottle collection here, and this is definitely in my top 10, maybe top 5.<br />
When I put this on, I know I'm going to smell incredible all day. It is such a calming "zen" scent and is a confidence booster to me. It smells like walking into a luxury spa. There's cucumber water, fresh fruits, a touch of tea, and maybe a hint of floral. One YouTuber said it gives him a "detox" vibe, and I definitely get that. It's unisex, slightly leaning feminine.<br />
Absolutely incredible Spring/Summer fragrance that I never want to be without again. I'll even wear it a bit in cooler weather, particularly if I'm going to be indoors. I mean... who doesn't want to smell a trip to the spa while at the office. I literally cannot stop bringing my wrist to my nose when I wear this; it's so addictive.<br />
My first impression, I put this at a 7/10. But now, I've been swayed. I've tried to be more conservative on my ratings, and I'm going to put this at a 9.8/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81423"comment_id="2145113"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Pacific-Chill-81423.html?ccid=2145113#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2142912" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1598503">Maliken</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-20">04/20/24 18:02</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Intense, vibrant fruitiness with a minty, slightly green undertone. I think the color of the bottle represents the scent quite well. It almost smells like a fruit cocktail; that intense fruity sweetness reaching candy-like levels of something you would smell in your average Paco Rabanne or Jean Paul Gaultier scent which I would normally find obnoxious, but unlike those aforementioned examples Pacific Chill somehow manages to avoid smelling like complete artificial crap. I don't think it necessarily pivots either to a  feminine or masculine direction, but it does smell rather youthful due to the prominent sweet smell.<br />
<br />
Pacific Chill smells like a designer scent at its core, a few notches elevated in quality but whether or not that's worth a niche level price is certainly debatable. But whenever I am in the mood for a sweet, fruity scent that doesn't turn into a cloying mess in the high heat of summer, this is my #1 choice.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; The only problem is its longevity. While it projects really really well for about 1 hour it then sits close on your skin but only for about 4 hours until its gone completely. It also isn't for everyone, it is definitely a very fruity fragrance and not everyone views that as a positive. When I asked my friends for their opinions some said it was a good citrusy fragrance that they liked and some said it smelled like a soapy apricot. For me this is a perfect summer fragrance but definitely do not blind buy.<br />
<br />
Price: 4/10 ($320)<br />
Longevity: 4/10 (doesn't last at all)<br />
Projection: 4/10 (projects really nicely but only for like 30 mins)<br />
Smell: 9/10 (citrusy and fresh)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="81423"comment_id="2126365"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Pacific-Chill-81423.html?ccid=2126365#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2124867" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
Opens very fruity and tropical, with a little bit of citrus from the lemon / citron. Compared to Afternoon Swim though I'd say this concentrates more on the tropical fruits with the Apricot being quite prominent for most of the wear, while Afternoon swim is more citrus heavy and not much else. For that reason I find this a lot more interesting. <br />
<br />
The mint is not in your face, but does its job well by bringing a cool feeling to the fruits, so that they don't become sickly and annoying.<br />
<br />
Overall 9/10.<br />
<br />
 Minus a point as I think the price is steep for a fragrance of this scent profile, but I understand that LV have a luxury brand image to uphold and probably use very high quality ingredients, which is obvious when smelling this.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; <br />
